def is_connected():
    try:
        import socket
        socket.create_connection(("1.1.1.1", 53))
        return True
    except OSError:
        pass
    return False

# thanh ngang


def thanh(so):
    a = "────"*so
    for i in range(len(a)):
        sys.stdout.write(a[i])
        sys.stdout.flush()
        sleep(0.003)
    print()
